***подложить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подложить.html>подложи́ть</a> (9045)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ложи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подложить.html>подложи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podložítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкладывать.html>подкла́дывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lay <i>(under)</i>, to put <i>(under)</i></li>
<li>to line <i>(with)</i></li>
<li>to add, to put some more
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подложить.html>подложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дрова.html>дро́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podložítʹ</b> drov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to add some firewood</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to put/place furtively, to plant
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подложить.html>подложи́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:наркотик.html>нарко́тики</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>podložíli</b> narkótiki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">drugs were planted on him</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подложить.html>подложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свинья.html>свинью́</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podložítʹ</b> svinʹjú komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to play a mean/dirty trick on/upon someone; do the dirty on someone</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***подлый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подлый.html>по́длый</a> (5441)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*podьlъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подлый.html>по́длый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pódlyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)подле́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:подлить.html>подле́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mean, low, dishonest, foul, dirty, bad</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подмастерье.html>подмасте́рье</a> (20682)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подмастерье.html>подмасте́рье</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podmastérʹje</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подмастерье.html>подмасте́рья</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подмастерье.html>подмасте́рья</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подмастерье.html>подмасте́рьев</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подменявший.html>подменя́вший</a> (18577)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подменявший.html>подменя́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podmenjávšij</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подметать.html>подмета́ющий</a> (18838)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мигнуть.html>мигну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mignútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

Grossman">Vasily Semyonovich Grossman</a>),  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>Жизнь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:судьба.html>судьба́</a></cite>, part 1, chapter class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">— <a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́й</a>, глушко́в, <a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>беги́</a> <a href = <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́л</a> глушко́в.<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:перебегать.html>перебега́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвым</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:опасный.html>опа́сное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:считаться.html>счита́лось</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:привилегия.html>привиле́гией</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:начальник.html>нача́льников</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:немец.html>не́мцы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обычно.html>обы́чно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:успевать.html>успева́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:открыть.html>откры́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>ого́нь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = Gluškóv.<br />Perebegátʹ pérvym opásnoje mésto sčitálosʹ privilégijej načálʹnikov, némcy obýčno ne uspeváli otkrýtʹ ogónʹ po pérvomu begúščemu.<br />Berjózkin ogljanúlsja na neméckije domá, <b>podmignúl</b> Gluškovu i pobežal.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">'You go first, Glushkov.'<br />'What do you mean? There's sure to be a sniper.'<br />It was a superior's privilege to be the first to cross a dangerous spot; usually the Germans were too slow to open fire straight away.<br />Byerozkin glanced round at the houses occupied by the Germans, <b>winked</b> at Glushkov and ran.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
